Motivation: 研究动机是测试大型语言模型在人类反馈训练下，是否会因为投资者已经对欺诈机会产生兴趣而抑制欺诈警告。担心AI可能会迎合用户的偏见，从而减少对欺诈投资的警告。

Method: 采用预注册实验设计，测试了7个领先的LLM和12个投资场景（包括合法、高风险和客观欺诈机会）。结合了3,360次AI咨询对话和1,201名参与者的基准人类数据，比较了AI和人类在投资咨询中的表现。

Result: 与预期相反，投资者的动机框架并没有抑制AI的欺诈警告，反而可能略微增加了警告频率。支持逆转的发生率低于千分之三。人类顾问在基准情况下有13-14%的欺诈投资支持率，而所有LLM都是0%。人类在压力下抑制警告的比率是AI的2-4倍。

Conclusion: 目前AI系统在相同的咨询角色中，比普通人类提供了更一致的欺诈警告。AI在识别和警告欺诈投资方面表现优于人类顾问，不会因为投资者的偏见而抑制警告。

Abstract: Large language models trained on human feedback may suppress fraud warnings when investors arrive already persuaded of a fraudulent opportunity. We tested this in a preregistered experiment across seven leading LLMs and twelve investment scenarios covering legitimate, high-risk, and objectively fraudulent opportunities, combining 3,360 AI advisory conversations with a 1,201-participant human benchmark. Contrary to predictions, motivated investor framing did not suppress AI fraud warnings; if anything, it marginally increased them. Endorsement reversal occurred in fewer than 3 in 1,000 observations. Human advisors endorsed fraudulent investments at baseline rates of 13-14%, versus 0% across all LLMs, and suppressed warnings under pressure at two to four times the AI rate. AI systems currently provide more consistent fraud warnings than lay humans in an identical advisory role.

</details>


### [167] [Learning to Evolve: A Self-Improving Framework for Multi-Agent Systems via Textual Parameter Graph Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20714)
*Shan He,Runze Wang,Zhuoyun Du,Huiyu Bai,Zouying Cao,Yu Cheng,Bo Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TPGO框架通过将多智能体系统建模为文本参数图，使用文本梯度和元学习策略实现系统的自我进化优化


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动优化方法主要关注平面提示调优，缺乏对多智能体系统复杂交互的结构感知能力，且优化器是静态的，无法从经验中学习改进优化策略

Method: 1) 将MAS建模为文本参数图(TPG)，其中智能体、工具和工作流是可优化的模块化节点；2) 从执行轨迹中提取"文本梯度"作为结构化自然语言反馈；3) 提出组相对智能体优化(GRAO)元学习策略，从历史优化经验中学习

Result: 在GAIA和MCP-Universe等复杂基准测试中，TPGO显著提升了最先进智能体框架的性能，通过自动化、自我改进的优化实现了更高的成功率

Conclusion: TPGO框架通过结构感知的建模、文本梯度反馈和元学习优化策略，使多智能体系统能够学习如何自我进化，解决了现有优化方法在复杂MAS中的局限性

Abstract: Designing and optimizing multi-agent systems (MAS) is a complex, labor-intensive process of "Agent Engineering." Existing automatic optimization methods, primarily focused on flat prompt tuning, lack the structural awareness to debug the intricate web of interactions in MAS. More critically, these optimizers are static; they do not learn from experience to improve their own optimization strategies. To address these gaps, we introduce Textual Parameter Graph Optimization (TPGO), a framework that enables a multi-agent system to learn to evolve. TPGO first models the MAS as a Textual Parameter Graph (TPG), where agents, tools, and workflows are modular, optimizable nodes. To guide evolution, we derive "textual gradients," structured natural language feedback from execution traces, to pinpoint failures and suggest granular modifications. The core of our framework is Group Relative Agent Optimization (GRAO), a novel meta-learning strategy that learns from historical optimization experiences. By analyzing past successes and failures, GRAO becomes progressively better at proposing effective updates, allowing the system to learn how to optimize itself. Extensive experiments on complex benchmarks like GAIA and MCP-Universe show that TPGO significantly enhances the performance of state-of-the-art agent frameworks, achieving higher success rates through automated, self-improving optimization.

### [168] [Interval POMDP Shielding for Imperfect-Perception Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20728)
*William Scarbro,Ravi Mangal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种基于置信区间的运行时防护机制，通过有限标注数据估计感知不确定性，构建区间部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程模型，为自主系统提供有限时域安全保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主系统依赖学习感知可能因传感器读数误分类而做出不安全决策，需要防护机制在运行时阻止可能违反安全性的动作。

Method: 从有限标注数据构建感知结果概率的置信区间，将系统建模为离散状态和动作的区间部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，提出算法计算与观测一致的保守信念集。

Result: 构建的运行时防护机制提供有限时域安全保证：在训练数据的高概率下，若真实感知不确定性率在学习的区间内，则防护允许的每个动作都满足安全下界。四个案例研究表明该方法优于现有基线。

Conclusion: 提出的基于置信区间的防护方法能有效提升依赖学习感知的自主系统的安全性，通过有限数据估计不确定性并提供可证明的安全保证。

Abstract: Autonomous systems that rely on learned perception can make unsafe decisions when sensor readings are misclassified. We study shielding for this setting: given a proposed action, a shield blocks actions that could violate safety. We consider the common case where system dynamics are known but perception uncertainty must be estimated from finite labeled data. From these data we build confidence intervals for the probabilities of perception outcomes and use them to model the system as a finite Interval Partially Observable Markov Decision Process with discrete states and actions. We then propose an algorithm to compute a conservative set of beliefs over the underlying state that is consistent with the observations seen so far.
  This enables us to construct a runtime shield that comes with a finite-horizon guarantee: with high probability over the training data, if the true perception uncertainty rates lie within the learned intervals, then every action admitted by the shield satisfies a stated lower bound on safety. Experiments on four case studies show that our shielding approach (and variants derived from it) improves the safety of the system over state-of-the-art baselines.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SiPeR框架，包含两个核心机制：1) 场景转换估计，评估当前场景是否满足用户需求，必要时引导用户到更合适的场景；2) 贝叶斯逆推理，利用多模态大语言模型的可能性预测用户在场景中对候选项目的偏好。

Result: 在两个代表性基准测试上的广泛实验表明，SiPeR在推荐准确性和响应生成质量方面均表现出优越性。

Abstract: Situated conversational recommendation (SCR), which utilizes visual scenes grounded in specific environments and natural language dialogue to deliver contextually appropriate recommendations, has emerged as a promising research direction due to its close alignment with real-world scenarios. Compared to traditional recommendations, SCR requires a deeper understanding of dynamic and implicit user preferences, as the surrounding scene often influences users' underlying interests, while both may evolve across conversations. This complexity significantly impacts the timing and relevance of recommendations. To address this, we propose situated preference reasoning (SiPeR), a novel framework that integrates two core mechanisms: (1) Scene transition estimation, which estimates whether the current scene satisfies user needs, and guides the user toward a more suitable scene when necessary; and (2) Bayesian inverse inference, which leverages the likelihood of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) to predict user preferences about candidate items within the scene. Extensive experiments on two representative benchmarks demonstrate SiPeR's superiority in both recommendation accuracy and response generation quality. The code and data are available at https://github.com/DongdingLin/SiPeR.

### [170] [V-tableR1: Process-Supervised Multimodal Table Reasoning with Critic-Guided Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20755)
*Yubo Jiang,Yitong An,Xin Yang,Abudukelimu Wuerkaixi,Xuxin Cheng,Fengying Xie,Zhiguo Jiang,Cao Liu,Ke Zeng,Haopeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: V-tableR1是一个基于过程监督强化学习的框架，通过表格结构作为视觉测试平台，训练多模态大语言模型进行可验证的推理，显著提升推理准确性并减少幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大语言模型仅基于最终结果训练，将视觉推理视为黑箱，依赖表面模式匹配而非严谨的多步推理。虽然可验证奖励的强化学习可以强制透明推理轨迹，但将其扩展到视觉领域面临将抽象逻辑映射到连续像素空间的模糊性问题。

Method: 利用表格的确定性网格结构作为理想视觉测试平台。V-tableR1采用专门的批评者VLM对策略VLM生成的显式视觉思维链提供密集的步骤级反馈。优化系统使用过程引导直接对齐策略优化（PGPO），这是一种整合过程奖励、解耦策略约束和长度感知动态采样的新型RL算法。

Result: V-tableR1明确惩罚视觉幻觉和捷径猜测。通过将多模态推理从黑箱模式匹配转变为可验证的逻辑推导，V-tableR1 4B在复杂表格基准测试中建立了开源模型的最先进准确性，性能超过其18倍大小的模型，并显著优于其SFT基线。

Conclusion: V-tableR1通过过程监督强化学习框架，成功将多模态推理从黑箱模式匹配转变为可验证的逻辑推导，在表格推理任务上取得了突破性进展，为视觉推理的透明性和准确性提供了新方法。

Abstract: We introduce V-tableR1, a process-supervised reinforcement learning framework that elicits rigorous, verifiable reasoning from multimodal large language models (MLLMs). Current MLLMs trained solely on final outcomes often treat visual reasoning as a black box, relying on superficial pattern matching rather than performing rigorous multi-step inference. While Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards could enforce transparent reasoning trajectories, extending it to visual domains remains severely hindered by the ambiguity of grounding abstract logic into continuous pixel space. We solve this by leveraging the deterministic grid structure of tables as an ideal visual testbed. V-tableR1 employs a specialized critic VLM to provide dense, step-level feedback on the explicit visual chain-of-thought generated by a policy VLM. To optimize this system, we propose Process-Guided Direct Alignment Policy Optimization (PGPO), a novel RL algorithm integrating process rewards, decoupled policy constraints, and length-aware dynamic sampling. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that V-tableR1 explicitly penalizes visual hallucinations and shortcut guessing. By fundamentally shifting multimodal inference from black-box pattern matching to verifiable logical derivation, V-tableR1 4B establishes state-of-the-art accuracy among open-source models on complex tabular benchmarks, outperforming models up to 18x its size and improving over its SFT baseline

### [171] [Diagnosing CFG Interpretation in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20811)
*Hanqi Li,Lu Chen,Kai Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLMs在解释上下文无关文法时存在层次性退化：表面语法保持较好，但深层结构语义难以维持，特别是在递归深度和分支复杂度较高时表现崩溃。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM越来越多地集成到智能体系统中，它们需要遵循动态定义的机器可解释接口。研究LLM作为上下文解释器的能力：给定新的上下文无关文法，LLM能否生成语法有效、行为功能正确且语义忠实的结果？

Method: 引入RoboGrid框架，通过控制递归深度、表达式复杂度和表面风格的应力测试，分离语法、行为和语义三个维度。使用CoT推理进行部分缓解，并测试"Alien"词典来探究LLM的符号归纳能力。

Result: 发现一致的层次性退化：LLM通常能保持表面语法，但难以保持结构语义。CoT推理提供部分缓解，但在结构密度（特别是深度递归和高分支）下性能崩溃，极端深度时语义对齐消失。"Alien"词典测试显示LLM依赖关键词的语义引导而非纯符号归纳。

Conclusion: 这些发现指出了可靠、文法无关智能体所需的分层状态跟踪存在关键差距，LLM在解释复杂文法结构时存在根本性限制。

Abstract: As LLMs are increasingly integrated into agentic systems, they must adhere to dynamically defined, machine-interpretable interfaces. We evaluate LLMs as in-context interpreters: given a novel context-free grammar, can LLMs generate syntactically valid, behaviorally functional, and semantically faithful outputs? We introduce RoboGrid, a framework that disentangles syntax, behavior, and semantics through controlled stress-tests of recursion depth, expression complexity, and surface styles. Our experiments reveal a consistent hierarchical degradation: LLMs often maintain surface syntax but fail to preserve structural semantics. Despite the partial mitigation provided by CoT reasoning, performance collapses under structural density, specifically deep recursion and high branching, with semantic alignment vanishing at extreme depths. Furthermore, "Alien" lexicons reveal that LLMs rely on semantic bootstrapping from keywords rather than pure symbolic induction. These findings pinpoint critical gaps in hierarchical state-tracking required for reliable, grammar-agnostic agents.

### [172] [Finite-Length Empirical Comparison of Polar, PAC, and Invertible-Extractor Secrecy Codes over the Wiretap BSC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19909)
*Jaswanthi Mandalapu,Andrew Thangaraj*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 比较三种有限码长下退化窃听二进制对称信道的保密编码方案：极化窃听陪集码、PAC窃听陪集码和可逆提取器框架，使用语义保密度量进行实证比较，发现PAC码在保持极化码保密性能的同时显著提高了可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限码长条件下，比较不同窃听信道保密编码方案的性能，特别是评估极化码、PAC码和可逆提取器框架在语义保密性和可靠性方面的表现，为实际系统设计提供指导。

Method: 1) 对极化陪集码，通过Tal-Vardy构造计算Eve的极化比特信道容量，获得互信息泄露的有限长度上界；2) 对PAC陪集码，证明其合成比特信道与极化码等价（至多置换），从而应用相同泄露界；3) 对可逆提取器框架，使用已有文献中的闭式语义保密界；4) 通过实证比较联合评估语义保密保证和Bob端的帧错误率性能。

Result: 1) PAC码在不改变极化码继承的保密界的情况下显著提高了可靠性；2) 在考虑的有限长度界下，极化/PAC保密码比可逆提取器框架提供更紧的保密保证；3) 证明了PAC码的合成比特信道与极化码等价，使得强保密界可转换为对称窃听信道的语义保密保证。

Conclusion: PAC窃听陪集码在有限码长条件下表现出优越性能，既保持了极化码的强保密特性，又通过路径选择显著提高了可靠性，为实际窃听信道保密通信提供了有前景的编码方案。

Abstract: We compare three secrecy-coding schemes for the degraded wiretap binary symmetric channel (BSC) in the finite-blocklength regime: (i) polar wiretap coset codes, (ii) PAC codes used as wiretap coset codes, and (iii) the invertible-extractor (IE) framework of Bellare-Tessaro. Our comparison is empirical and uses a common semantic-secrecy metric (distinguishing advantage). For polar coset codes, we compute Eve's polarized bit-channel capacities (via the Tal-Vardy construction) to obtain explicit finite-length upper bounds on mutual-information leakage, yielding strong secrecy bounds. For PAC coset codes, we prove that Eve's synthesized bit-channels are equivalent to those of polar codes (up to a permutation), so the same leakage bounds apply; we then convert these strong-secrecy bounds into semantic-secrecy guarantees for symmetric wiretap channels. For the IE scheme, we use the closed-form semantic-secrecy bounds given in the reference work. Finally, we report finite-length results that jointly characterize (a) semantic-secrecy guarantees against Eve and (b) frame-error-rate performance at Bob, illustrating that PAC codes can significantly improve reliability without changing the secrecy bounds inherited from polar coding. Moreover, under the finite-length bounds considered in this work, polar/PAC secrecy codes provide tighter security guarantees than the invertible-extractor framework.

</details>


### [173] [Robust Uniform Recovery of Structured Signals from Nonlinear Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20075)
*Pedro Abdalla,Radu Balan,Junren Chen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于受限近似可逆性条件(RAIC)的统一框架，用于从非线性观测中实现结构化信号的均匀恢复，证明了投影梯度下降(PGD)在RAIC条件下能够实现均匀恢复，并在多种稀疏恢复场景中达到了与非均匀恢复相同的误差阶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然受限等距性质(RIP)保证了从含噪线性测量中均匀稀疏恢复，但从非线性观测中均匀恢复结构化信号的研究仍然不足。本文旨在填补这一空白，为非线性观测下的均匀恢复提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 提出使用受限近似可逆性条件(RAIC)作为统一方法，证明投影梯度下降(PGD)在梯度满足RAIC条件时能够实现均匀恢复。通过覆盖论证建立了高斯单指标模型下均匀RAIC，并使用VC维论证处理1-bit量化非线性情况。

Result: 在多种稀疏恢复场景中，均匀恢复的误差率与非均匀恢复的误差率相同（最多相差对数因子）。特别地，在1-bit量化非线性下，迭代硬阈值(IHT)的均匀恢复误差与非均匀恢复误差同阶且无对数因子损失。结果改进了Genzel和Stollenwerk(2023)的工作。

Conclusion: RAIC为非线性观测下的均匀恢复提供了有效的统一框架，PGD在RAIC条件下能够实现均匀恢复，且在多种实际稀疏恢复场景中达到了最优的误差率。该方法还能优雅地处理噪声和损坏的鲁棒性问题。

Abstract: While it is well known that the restricted isometry property (RIP) guarantees uniform sparse recovery from noisy linear measurements, uniform recovery of structured signals from nonlinear observations remains much less understood. This paper shows that the restricted approximate invertibility condition (RAIC) provides a unified approach to this end. Particularly, uniform recovery is achieved by projected gradient descent (PGD) with gradients obeying RAIC for all signals. As an application, under a large class of piecewise Lipschitz link functions (possibly discontinuous), we develop a uniform recovery theory for Gaussian single-index model by establishing the uniform RAIC for the gradient of the (scaled) $\ell_2$ loss via a covering argument. The theory generalizes the nonuniform recovery guarantees due to Plan and Vershynin (2016); Oymak and Soltanolkotabi (2017) and exhibits additional error terms that can be interpreted as the cost of uniform recovery. Intriguingly, in the three canonical settings of (a) sparse recovery via PGD with $\ell_0$ projection (i.e., iterative hard thresholding (IHT)), (b) sparse recovery via PGD with $\ell_1$ projection, and (c) recovering approximately sparse signals via PGD with $\ell_1$ projection, the additional error terms are negligible and in turn our uniform recovery error rates are at the same order of existing nonuniform ones, up to log factors. Our results hence improve on Genzel and Stollenwerk (2023). Under the specific nonlinearity of 1-bit quantization, we use a VC dimension argument to show that the uniform recovery error of IHT is at the same order of the nonuniform recovery error, with no loss of log factor. In addition, we show that the robustness of PGD to noise and corruption can be incorporated elegantly by bounding a single additional random process that captures the gradient mismatch.

</details>


### [174] [Secure Rate-Distortion-Perception: A Randomized Distributed Function Computation Approach for Realism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20245)
*Gustaf Åhlgren,Onur Günlü*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在需要保持重建数据感知质量的应用中的安全率失真感知（RDP）权衡问题，特别是在有信息泄露风险的情况下。论文分析了无噪声信道和广播信道的安全RDP性能，推导了精确的安全RDP区域，并证明了随机分箱编码能同时实现强保密性、低失真和高感知质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在神经图像压缩等需要保持重建数据感知质量的应用中，存在基本的率失真感知（RDP）权衡。当压缩数据通过公共通信信道传输时，会出现安全风险。因此，研究在无噪声信道和具有相关噪声分量的广播信道（BCs）上，信息泄露可忽略情况下的安全RDP问题具有重要意义。

Method: 论文采用信息论方法研究安全RDP问题。对于无噪声信道，精确刻画了安全RDP区域。对于广播信道，推导了内界，并证明对于一类更强大的广播信道是紧的。进一步证明了当有无限公共随机性可用时，分离的源信道编码对于这个精确的安全RDP区域是最优的。此外，当编码器和解码器都能访问与源相关的边信息且信道无噪声时，建立了精确的RDP区域。如果只有解码器在无噪声设置中有相关边信息，推导了内界以及区域精确的特殊情况。

Result: 论文的主要结果包括：1）无噪声信道下精确的安全RDP区域表征；2）广播信道下的内界，并证明对一类更强大的广播信道是紧的；3）证明分离源信道编码在无限公共随机性下的最优性；4）建立编码器和解码器都有相关边信息时的精确RDP区域；5）推导只有解码器有边信息时的内界和精确特殊情况。二进制和高斯示例表明，与标准率失真设置不同，公共随机性能显著降低安全RDP设置中的通信速率。

Conclusion: 随机分箱编码能够同时实现强保密性、低失真和高感知质量。研究结果表明，在安全RDP设置中，公共随机性可以显著降低通信速率，这与标准率失真设置不同。论文为需要在保持感知质量的同时确保数据安全的应用提供了理论基础和实用指导。

Abstract: Fundamental rate-distortion-perception (RDP) trade-offs arise in applications requiring maintained perceptual quality of reconstructed data, such as neural image compression. When compressed data is transmitted over public communication channels, security risks emerge. We therefore study secure RDP under negligible information leakage over both noiseless channels and broadcast channels, BCs, with correlated noise components. For noiseless channels, the exact secure RDP region is characterized. For BCs, an inner bound is derived and shown to be tight for a class of more-capable BCs. Separate source-channel coding is further shown to be optimal for this exact secure RDP region with unlimited common randomness available. Moreover, when both encoder and decoder have access to side information correlated with the source and the channel is noiseless, the exact RDP region is established. If only the decoder has correlated side information in the noiseless setting, an inner bound is derived along with a special case where the region is exact. Binary and Gaussian examples demonstrate that common randomness can significantly reduce the communication rate in secure RDP settings, unlike in standard rate-distortion settings. Thus, our results illustrate that random binning-based coding achieves strong secrecy, low distortion, and high perceptual quality simultaneously.

</details>


### [175] [Trajectory Design for Fairness Enhancement in Movable Antennas-Aided Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20364)
*Guojie Hu,Qingqing Wu,Lipeng Zhu,Kui Xu,Guoxin Li,Tong-Xing Zheng*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了多用户上行通信系统中可移动天线(MA)的轨迹设计问题，旨在通过优化基站天线轨迹来最大化所有用户的最小可达速率，提升系统公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可移动天线技术能够通过自适应天线重新定位来按需重构无线信道，为提升通信性能创造了额外的空间自由度。然而，优化的阵列几何结构无法保证速率公平性，因此需要设计天线轨迹来最大化所有用户的最小可达速率。

Method: 首先研究理想情况（无限快天线移动），通过拉格朗日对偶方法最优求解；然后在有限移动速度的一般情况下，基于理想场景识别的最优模式提出启发式轨迹设计；最后通过简化特例获得更多洞见。

Result: 研究发现基站应使用有限组天线部署模式，每个模式分配最优时间持续时间。基于此，提出了适用于有限移动速度的启发式轨迹设计，并通过数值结果验证了所提设计相比竞争基准的有效性。

Conclusion: 可移动天线轨迹设计能够有效提升多用户上行通信系统的公平性，特别是在有限移动速度约束下，基于理想最优模式启发的设计方法具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Through adaptive antenna repositioning, the movable antenna (MA) technology enables on-demand reconfiguration of wireless channels, thereby creating an additional spatial degree of freedom in improving communication performance. This paper investigates a multiuser uplink communication system aided by MAs, where a base station (BS) equipped with multiple MAs serves multiple single-antenna users. Specifically, given that an optimized array geometry cannot guarantee rate fairness, we focus on designing antenna trajectory at the BS to maximize the minimum achievable rate among all users over a finite time period. The resulting optimization problem is fundamentally challenging to solve due to the continuous-time nature. To address it, we first examine an ideal case with infinitely fast MA movement and demonstrate that the relaxed problem can be optimally solved via the Lagrangian dual method. The obtained trajectory solution reveals that the BS should employ a finite set of MA deployment patterns, each allocated an optimal time duration. Building on this, we then study the general case with limited MA movement speed and propose a heuristic trajectory design inspired by the optimal patterns identified in the ideal scenario. Several insights are also gained by examining the simplified special case. Finally, numerical results are provided to validate the effectiveness of the proposed designs compared to competitive benchmarks.

### [176] [Rate-Cost Tradeoffs in Nonlinear Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20369)
*Eray Unsal Atay,Venkat Chandrasekaran,Victoria Kostina*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了有限时域内一般随机控制系统（包括非线性系统）在速率受限控制中的速率-成本权衡，建立了最小可达通信速率与有向信息最小化问题之间的非渐近界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一般随机控制系统（包括非线性系统）在有限时域内速率受限控制中的基本极限，扩展有向信息在因果信源编码和LQG控制之外的应用范围。

Method: 在每个时间步，编码器观察状态并传输描述给控制器，控制器选择控制动作。通过构建使用强函数表示引理的编码控制策略，证明了上界。

Result: 对于平均控制成本阈值D，最小可达通信速率R_n(D)位于有向信息最小化问题F_n(D)的对数加性间隙内：F_n(D) ≤ R_n(D) ≤ F_n(D) + log(F_n(D)+3.4) + 2 + 1/n（比特）。

Conclusion: 有向信息是控制速率受限控制的操作相关量，将其应用从因果信源编码和LQG控制扩展到一般非线性控制系统，并为顺序（因果）率失真和LQG控制提供了非渐近界。

Abstract: We study the rate-cost tradeoff in rate-limited control of general stochastic control systems, including nonlinear systems, over a finite horizon. At each time step, an encoder observes the state and transmits a description to a controller, which then selects the control action. For an average control-cost threshold $D$, we characterize the minimum achievable communication rate $R_n(D)$ via a nonasymptotic bound: $R_n(D)$ lies within an additive logarithmic gap of the optimal value of a directed-information minimization $F_n(D)$, namely, we show that $F_n(D) \le R_n(D) \le F_n(D)+\log \bigl(F_n(D)+3.4\bigr)+2+\frac{1}{n}$, in bits. This establishes directed information as the operationally relevant quantity governing rate-limited control, thereby broadening its utility beyond its previously established roles in causal source coding and linear quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control to general nonlinear control systems. We prove the upper bound constructively by building an encoding-and-control policy using the strong functional representation lemma at each time step. As special cases of our setting, our framework yields nonasymptotic bounds for sequential (causal) rate-distortion and LQG control.

</details>


### [177] [CSI Feedback Under Basis Mismatch: Rate-Splitting Transform Coding for FDD Massive MIMO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20380)
*Youngmok Park,Bumsu Park,Namyoon Lee*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出一种分离长期基反馈与短期系数量化的实用架构，解决大规模MIMO系统中KL变换基失配问题，实现近最优性能并显著降低复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在频分双工大规模MIMO系统中，下行信道状态信息必须在有限的上行预算内反馈。虽然基于Karhunen-Loeve变换和反向注水算法的变换编码对高斯信道是率失真最优的，但其性能受到用户与基站之间基失配的限制。

Method: 提出一种实用架构，将长期基反馈与短期系数量化分离。使用随机矢量量化推导出端到端均方误差的闭式表达式，从而表征最优速率分配并识别基更新的相变阈值。

Result: 在相关高斯信道和COST2100信道上的仿真表明，该方法实现了近最优性能，对更新开销具有鲁棒性，并且相比基于深度学习的自编码器显著降低了复杂度。

Conclusion: 通过分离长期基反馈和短期系数量化，有效解决了大规模MIMO系统中KL变换基失配问题，实现了性能与复杂度的良好平衡。

Abstract: In frequency division duplex massive multiple-input multiple-output systems, downlink channel state information must be fed back within a limited uplink budget. While transform coding with Karhunen-Loeve transform and reverse water-filling is rate-distortion optimal for Gaussian channels, its performance is limited by basis mismatch between the user and base station. We analyze this mismatch and propose a practical architecture separating long-term basis feedback from short-term coefficient quantization. Using a random vector quantization, we derive a closed-form end-to-end mean square error expression. This allows us to characterize the optimal rate split and identify a phase transition threshold for basis updates. Simulations on correlated Gaussian and COST2100 channels demonstrate near-optimal performance, robustness to update overhead, and significant complexity reduction compared to deep-learning-based autoencoders.

### [178] [Fundamental Tradeoff in Movable Antenna Systems: How Long to Move Before Transmission?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20386)
*Guojie Hu,Qingqing Wu,Lipeng Zhu,Shanpu Shen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究可移动天线技术中天线移动时间与数据传输时间之间的权衡，通过联合优化移动时间和天线部署来最大化有效吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可移动天线技术通过自适应天线部署能够灵活重构无线信道，但天线移动需要时间，在此期间通信可能受到信道波动和多普勒效应的影响，导致移动时间与数据传输时间之间存在根本性权衡。

Method: 针对多用户下行链路场景，联合优化基站天线移动时间和部署位置以最大化有效吞吐量。提出拟合方法仅采样少量速率-持续时间对，获得闭式表达式捕捉速率趋势；推导天线最大移动速度的闭式条件。

Result: 当天线移动速度低于特定阈值时，最优策略是在整个传输期间保持天线静止。通过两个可移动天线和两个用户的特殊案例验证了基本权衡和所提方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 数值仿真验证了所提方案的有效性，揭示了可移动天线系统中移动时间与传输时间之间的基本权衡，为实际系统设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: The movable antenna (MA) technology enables flexible reconfiguration of wireless channels through adaptive antenna deployment, offering significant potential for enhancing communication performance. However, antenna movement requires a certain duration within which communication may be compromised due to factors such as channel fluctuation and Doppler effect. This leads to a fundamental tradeoff: A longer movement duration allows antennas to reach more favorable positions for better channel conditions, but it inevitably reduces the time available for data transmission. To characterize the aforementioned tradeoff, we focus on the MAs-enabled multiuser downlink scenario, and jointly optimize the movement duration and antenna deployment at the base station to maximize the effective throughput. The formulated problem is highly non-convex. The general solutions require an one-dimensional search over movement durations, each with optimized antenna deployment. To reduce complexity, we propose a fitting method that samples only a few rate-duration pairs, yielding a closed-form expression that captures the rate trend and enables a favorable solution immediately. We further derive a closed-form condition on the maximum antenna movement speed: When the speed is below a certain threshold, the optimal strategy is to keep antennas stationary throughout the transmission period. The fundamental tradeoff and the effectiveness of the proposed solutions are examined in a special case with two MAs and two users. Finally, numerical simulations validate the efficacy of the proposed schemes.

Abstract: Direct satellite uplink is severely constrained by limited link budgets, which hinder the exploitation of wideband resources, and ultimately limit the throughout. ### [182] [DNA storage approaching the information-theoretic ceiling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20810)
*James L. Banal*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种DNA存储编码方案，通过保留测序器的后验分布信息，实现了更高的存储密度和长期稳定性，接近香农极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成DNA具有极高的存储密度（227.5 EB/g）和千年尺度的稳定性，但实现这一容量需要能够从合成和测序错误中恢复数据的纠错码。现有编解码器将噪声测序输出转换为离散碱基调用后再纠错，丢弃了关于位置可靠性的概率信息。

Method: 提出了一种保留测序器每个位置后验分布的编码方案，采用集成解码器，包括轮廓隐马尔可夫模型对齐、跨读数的对数乘积融合和有序统计解码。

Result: 在DT4DDS通道模拟器上，该编解码器在高保真和低保真条件下分别恢复155.8和25.9 EB/g的dsDNA存储密度，比先前最佳技术分别提高11%和52%。在25°C干燥状态下基于脱嘌呤动力学的单编码降解协议中，预计可解码存储时间为282年，密度为17.1 EB/g。

Conclusion: 该编码方案使DNA存储密度接近底层通道的香农极限，为实现DNA存储的高密度和长期稳定性提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Synthetic DNA approaches 227.5 exabytes per gram of storage density with stability over millennial timescales. Realising this capacity requires error-correction codes that recover data from substantial synthesis and sequencing errors. Existing codecs convert noisy sequencer output into discrete base calls before error correction, discarding probabilistic information about which positions are reliable. Here we present a coding scheme that retains the sequencer's per-position posterior distributions through an integrated decoder of profile hidden Markov model alignment, log-product fusion across reads, and ordered-statistics decoding. On the DT4DDS channel simulator, the codec recovers 155.8 and 25.9 exabytes per gram of dsDNA under high- and low-fidelity conditions, exceeding the highest prior-art density on each channel by 11 and 52 percent. Under a single-encode-then-degrade protocol mapped to depurination kinetics at 25 °C in the dry state, the codec projects 282 years of decodable storage at 17.1 exabytes per gram. These results place DNA storage density within reach of the Shannon bound of the underlying channel.

</details>
